King of the Gypsies, directed by Frank Pierson and written by Peter Maas and Frank Pierson, takes us into the unforgiving world of modern-day Gypsies residing in New York City. The movie centers around Zharko Stepanowicz, the 'king' of this community, who bestows his position and authority to his unwilling grandson. As the father, who took a step back from the family, struggles with resentment, a dangerous game of power, influence, and loyalty unfolds.

Sweetwater" (2023) is a riveting biography that traces the journey of Nat "Sweetwater" Clifton, a groundbreaking figure in the history of basketball.
